country_event = { #Startup Event
	id = the_command.0
	title = the_command.0.t
	desc = the_command.0.d
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			4311 = {
				set_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 50
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = the_command.110
				days = 25
				random = 10
			}
			R63 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R64 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R65 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			R66 = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = all
				loyalty = 1
			}
			4628 = {
				set_province_flag = command_converted_province_flag
				change_culture = shamadhan
				change_religion = accretive_path
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = previousCulture
					value = culture
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = previousReligion
					value = religion
				}
				change_culture = brown_orc
				change_religion = old_dookan
			}
			4521 = {
				set_province_flag = command_converted_province_flag
				change_culture = khedarid
				change_religion = high_philosophy
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = previousCulture
					value = culture
				}
				export_to_variable = {
					variable_name = previousReligion
					value = religion
				}
				change_culture = brown_orc
				change_religion = old_dookan
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.0.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_army_professionalism = 0.2
		
		custom_tooltip = command_mechanics_hint_tt
	}
}

province_event = { # Orcish slaves in $Provincename$
	id = the_command.2
	title = the_command.2.t
	desc = the_command.2.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owned_by = R62
		continent = asia
		owner = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = the_abolish_slavery_act } }
		NOT = { fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = orcish } }
		NOT = {
			province_id = 5424
			has_terrain = city_terrain
			trade_goods = cloth
			trade_goods = paper
			trade_goods = glass
			trade_goods = chinaware
			trade_goods = slaves
			trade_goods = silk
			trade_goods = dyes
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				trade_goods = tea
				trade_goods = cotton
				trade_goods = spices
				trade_goods = tropical_wood
				trade_goods = tobacco
				trade_goods = sugar
				trade_goods = coffee
				trade_goods = iron
				trade_goods = copper
				trade_goods = gold
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = hobgoblin
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			OR = {
				trade_goods = grain
				trade_goods = livestock
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			unrest = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			unrest = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			unrest = 10
		}
	}
	is_mtth_scaled_to_size = 1

	option = { # 
		name = the_command.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = orcish_slave_boom
			duration = 3650
		}
		add_orcish_minority_size_effect = yes
		owner = { small_decrease_of_orcish_tolerance_effect = yes }
	}
}

country_event = { # The rule of [Root.Monarch.GetName]
	id = the_command.3
	title = the_command.3.t
	desc = the_command.3.desc
	picture = SEJM_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_wolf_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_wolf_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_boar_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_boar_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_lion_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_dragon_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_elephant_command_special_commissions
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_special_commissions_no_dlc }
				set_country_flag = revoke_tiger_command_special_commissions
			}
			set_country_flag = special_commission_cooldown_refresh
		}
	}

	option = { # The time of the Wolf has come
		name = the_command.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = R96
				has_estate = estate_wolf_command
			}
			NOT = { tag = R94 tag = R95 }
			OR = {
				dynasty = "Wolfborn"
				AND = {
					NOT = { dynasty = "Boarborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Lionborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Dragonborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Elephantborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Tigerborn" }
				}
			}
		}
		command_new_ruler_effect = { command = wolf }
	}

	option = { # The time of the Boar has come
		name = the_command.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = R94
				has_estate = estate_boar_command
			}
			NOT = { tag = R95 tag = R96 }
			OR = {
				dynasty = "Boarborn"
				AND = {
					NOT = { dynasty = "Wolfborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Lionborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Dragonborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Elephantborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Tigerborn" }
				}
			}
		}
		
		command_new_ruler_effect = { command = boar }
	}

	option = { # The time of the Lion has come
		name = the_command.3.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = R95
				has_estate = estate_lion_command
			}
			NOT = { tag = R94 tag = R96 }
			OR = {
				dynasty = "Lionborn"
				AND = {
					NOT = { dynasty = "Wolfborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Boarborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Dragonborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Elephantborn" }
					NOT = { dynasty = "Tigerborn" }
				}
			}
		}
		
		command_new_ruler_effect = { command = lion }
	}

	option = { # The time of the Dragon has come
		name = the_command.3.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = R69
				has_estate = estate_dragon_command
			}
			OR = {

	option = { # The time of the Elephant has come

### Magic events

country_event = { #End the Temple's Curse
	id = the_command.4
	title = the_command.4.t
	desc = the_command.4.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { OR = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex } NOT = { has_province_flag = temple_being_plundered } NOT = { has_province_modifier = temple_restoration_efforts } is_city = yes is_core = ROOT }
				setup_temple_restoration_speed = yes
				calculate_temple_restoration = yes
				save_event_target_as = restore1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = command_the_temples_curse_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { has_temple_complex = yes }
				add_ogre_minority_size_effect = yes
			}
		}
		event_target:restore1 = { begin_temple_restoration = yes }
		tooltip = {
			custom_tooltip = temple_restoration_cost_tt1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Betrayal of the Oni!
	id = the_command.7
	title = the_command.7.t
	desc = the_command.7.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = command_oni_temple_stewardship_flag
		is_year = 1608
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						has_province_modifier = temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
						has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = temple_complex }
					hidden_effect = {
						corrupt_temple_wards = yes
						set_province_flag = was_temple_complex
					}
					remove_province_modifier = temple_complex
					add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex }
					hidden_effect = {
						corrupt_temple_wards = yes
						set_province_flag = was_damaged_temple_complex
					}
					remove_province_modifier = damaged_temple_complex
					add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex }
					hidden_effect = {
						corrupt_temple_wards = yes
						set_province_flag = was_derelict_temple_complex
					}
					remove_province_modifier = derelict_temple_complex
					add_province_triggered_modifier = corrupted_temple_complex
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = command_oni_temple_stewardship_flag
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.7.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = command_the_oni_betrayal_tt
	}
}


### Jade Mines events

country_event = { #Goblin Infighting
	id = the_command.10
	title = the_command.10.t
	desc = the_command.10.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture
	goto = rebel_target

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
		NOT = { has_country_flag = command_jade_rivalry_ended }
		4311 = {
			check_variable = {
				which = command_jade_mines_tension
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 30
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 40
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			4311 = {
				check_variable = {
					which = command_jade_mines_tension
					value = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = { region = jade_mines_region }
				save_event_target_as = rebel_target
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		event_target:rebel_target = {
			spawn_dwarovar_goblin_rebels = { size = 1 }
		}
		
		# 4311 = {
			# change_variable = {
				# which = command_jade_mines_tension
				# value = 1
			# }
		# }
	}
}

### Moving Camp Events
### This event throws an error that says "undefined event target". Ignore it!!! It is not true!!!
province_event = { #Migration from X to Y
	id = the_command.20
	title = the_command.20.t
	desc = the_command.20.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture
	goto = command_destination_province

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = hobgoblin }
		country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = R62
	}

	#immediate is dangerous, try not to put too many things in there
	#tl;dr: if two of the same event happen their immediates fire but you don't see the second event.
	#it can also break loca and flags and suchlike. In this case it's fine tho
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { province_event = { id = the_command.20 days = 365 random = 730 } }
	}
	after = {
		command_migration_randomization_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.20.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		####Migration Away from Existing Camp
		if = {
			limit = { has_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes }
			remove_racial_minority_any_size = { race = hobgoblin }
		}
		else_if = { #3-dev provinces convert, or the holds do when they get small enough
			limit = {
				OR = { #province that's a 1 in something converts
					NOT = { base_tax = 2 }
					NOT = { base_production = 2 }
					NOT = { base_manpower = 2 }
					AND = { province_id = 4313 NOT = { development = 16 } } #Vurdriz-Andriz
					AND = { province_id = 4311 NOT = { development = 23 } } #Gronstunad
				}
			}
			change_culture = undergrowth_goblin
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = command_governed_by_undergrowth
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = { #subtract dev to get them low
			if = {
				limit = { base_tax = 2 }
				add_base_tax = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { base_production = 2 }
				add_base_production = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = { base_manpower = 2 }
				add_base_manpower = -1
			}
		}
		####Migration to New Camp
		event_target:command_destination_province = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = R62 } }
				#do nothing
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_large_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes }
				if = {
					limit = { owner = { num_of_owned_provinces_with = { value = 4 culture = lion_command region = shamakhad_region } } }
					random_list = {
						3 = { add_base_tax = 2 }
						3 = { add_base_production = 2 }
						4 = { add_base_manpower = 2 }
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						2 =  {
							random_list = {
								3 = { add_base_tax = 2 }
								3 = { add_base_production = 2 }
								4 = { add_base_manpower = 2 }
							}
						}
						1 = {
							change_culture = lion_command
							change_religion = godlost
							random_list = {
								3 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
								3 = { add_base_production = 1 }
								4 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_hobgoblin_majority_trigger = yes }
				random_list = {
					3 = { add_base_tax = 2 }
					3 = { add_base_production = 2 }
					4 = { add_base_manpower = 2 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_small_hobgoblin_minority_trigger = yes }
				generic_add_race_minority_size_effect = { race = hobgoblin }
				random_list = {
					3 = { add_base_tax = 1 }
					3 = { add_base_production = 1 }
					4 = { add_base_manpower = 1 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				generic_add_race_minority_size_effect = { race = hobgoblin }
				generic_add_race_minority_size_effect = { race = hobgoblin }
			}
		}
	}
}

province_event = { #The Laws of Ninun
	id = the_command.34
	title = the_command.34.t
	desc = the_command.34.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = { continent = serpentspine }
		owner = {
			OR = {
				tag = R62
				is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = {
					who = R62
					type = slave_state
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_state_edict = laws_of_ninun_edict
			has_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag
				is_state = yes
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = R62_slave_state_wuhyunification_flag
				owner = {
					is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = {
						who = R62
						type = slave_state
					}
				}
			}
		}
		command_not_yet_wuhyunized = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_proselytizers_to_the_wuhyun } }
			province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 110 random = 219 }
		}
		else = {
			province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 137 random = 274 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.34.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			culture_is_wuhyun = no
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_culture
				value = culture
				who = ROOT
			}
		} # for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				trigger = { has_orcish_majority_trigger = no }
				if = {
					limit = { has_harimari_majority_trigger = yes }
					change_culture = worthy_harimari
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_harpy_majority_trigger = yes }
					change_culture = reishao_harpy
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_kobold_majority_trigger = yes }
					change_culture = dragonfire_kobold
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_goblin_majority_trigger = yes }
					change_culture = march_goblin
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_elven_majority_trigger = yes }
					change_culture = sunset_elf
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { superregion = rahen_superregion }
					change_culture = azepyanunin
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							superregion = yanshen_superregion
							superregion = north_haless_superregion
						}
					}
					change_culture = ikaniwagain
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { superregion = south_haless_superregion }
					change_culture = kintonan
				}
				else = {
					change_culture = rinonokegyun
				}
			}
			2 = {
				trigger = {
					has_global_flag = R62_honourable_half_orcs_flag
					OR = {
						has_orcish_majority_trigger = yes
						has_any_half_orcish_pop_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				change_culture = wuhyun_half_orc
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.34.b
		trigger = { NOT = { religion = godlost } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		if = {
			limit = { continent = asia }
			export_to_variable = {
				which = original_wuhyun_religion
				value = religion
				who = ROOT
			}
		} # for sunrise empire to convert wuhyun back

		change_religion = godlost
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = command_not_yet_wuhyunized_mod
					command_not_yet_wuhyunized = no
				}
				remove_province_modifier = command_not_yet_wuhyunized_mod
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag }
					owner = { ai = yes }
					command_not_yet_wuhyunized = no
				}
				clr_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag
				every_neighbor_province = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag }
						command_not_yet_wuhyunized = yes
					}
					set_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag }
					owner = { ai = no }
					area_for_scope_province = {
						type = all
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_state_edict = laws_of_ninun_edict }
							AND = {
								religion = godlost
								culture_is_wuhyun = yes
							}
							culture_group_is_wuhyunizable = no
						}
					}
				}
				province_event = { id = the_command.55 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Tughayasa Petition
	id = the_command.44
	title = the_command.44.t
	desc = the_command.44.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	
	option = { #The War Room is full enough
		name = the_command.44.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					}
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
					}
					AND = {
						has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
						has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					}
				}
			}
			add_absolutism = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
					has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
				}
			}
			add_absolutism = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_absolutism = 15
		}
		
		clr_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	option = { #That concludes our meeting
		name = the_command.44.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
			has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
			has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		clr_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag
	}
	
	option = { #The Dragon Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights }}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_war_room_rights
		custom_tooltip = estate_command_unlock_war_room_tt
	}
	option = { #The Elephant Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights }}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_war_room_rights
		custom_tooltip = estate_command_unlock_war_room_tt
	}
	option = { #The Tiger Command earned their place
		name = the_command.44.d
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights }}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_war_room_rights
		custom_tooltip = estate_command_unlock_war_room_tt
	}
	
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = command_tughayasa_petition_open_flag }
			country_event = { id = the_command.4400 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A universal Command
	id = the_command.45
	title = the_command.45.t
	desc = the_command.45.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = the_command.45.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1650 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = command_the_edict
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1700 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = command_the_edict2
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_year = 1750 }
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = command_the_edict3
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = command_the_edict4
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				clr_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
				clr_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag
				if = {
					limit = { command_not_yet_wuhyunized = yes }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_not_yet_wuhyunized_mod
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag
		}
		custom_tooltip = desc_command_the_edict
	}
}

					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}

			}
			command_change_korashi_supply = { increase = yes }
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = command_slave_state_flag }
		}
		Y01 = {
			release_all_subjects = yes

		}

		}

		add_trust = {
			who = R62
			value = -40
			mutual = yes
		}
	}

country_event = { #Auto-Wuhyunification pulse
	id = the_command.51
	title = the_command.51.t
	desc = the_command.51.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag
				tag = R62
			}
			AND = {
				tag = R62
				mission_completed = R62_laws_of_ninun
				ai = yes
				NOT = { has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag }
			}
			AND = {
				has_global_flag = R62_slave_state_wuhyunification_flag
				is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = {
					who = R62
					type = slave_state
				}
				ai = yes
				OR = {
					tag = R63
					tag = R64
					tag = Y01
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.34.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag
			tag = R62
		}
		
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				is_state = yes
				has_province_modifier = command_not_yet_wuhyunized_mod
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_proselytizers_to_the_wuhyun } }
				province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 39 random = 438 }
			}
			else = {
				province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 94 random = 548 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.34.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = R62_slave_state_wuhyunification_flag
			is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = {
				who = R62
				type = slave_state
			}
		}

		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				is_state = yes
				command_not_yet_wuhyunized = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_proselytizers_to_the_wuhyun } }
				province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 39 random = 438 }
			}
			else = {
				province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 94 random = 548 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = flavor_castanor_go_back
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			tag = R62
			NOT = { has_global_flag = R62_the_edict_of_x_flag }
		}

		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
				NOT = { has_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag }
			}
			random_list = {
				7 = {
					clr_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
					set_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag
					if = {
						limit = { owner = { has_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_proselytizers_to_the_wuhyun } }
						province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 39 random = 438 }
					}
					else = {
						province_event = { id = the_command.34 days = 94 random = 548 }
					}
				}
				193 = {}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { is_year = 1600 }
			random_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					command_not_yet_wuhyunized = yes
					NOT = {
						has_province_flag = ai_command_currently_wuhyunizing_this_province_flag
						has_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = ai_command_wuhyunize_this_province_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Ruler Proves Leadership
	id = the_command.56
	title = the_command.56.t
	desc = the_command.56.desc
	picture = SEJM_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.56.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership }
			remove_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_respected_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = command_respected_leadership }
			remove_country_modifier = command_respected_leadership
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_legendary_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = command_legendary_leadership } }
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_exemplary_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_mil_power = 50
		}
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 5 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Rise of the Shamans Start
	id = the_command.80
	title = the_command.80.t
	desc = the_command.80.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -3
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = command_first_rise_of_shamans } }
				country_event = {
					id = the_command.82
					days = 31
				}
				country_event = {
					id = the_command.83
					days = 88
				}
				set_country_flag = command_first_rise_of_shamans
			}
		
			random_owned_province = {
				mage_rebels = 1
			}
			random_owned_province = {
				mage_rebels = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Flee! Flee for your lives!
		name = the_command.80.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		tooltip = {
			add_stability = -3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Chandra of the Many Hands comes out in the open
	id = the_command.84
	title = the_command.84.t
	desc = the_command.84.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { R09 = { exists = no } 4467 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
					
					4467 = {
						add_core = R09
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R09
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R09
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R09 religion = high_philosophy culture = rajnadhid }
					R09 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { R12 = { exists = no } 4509 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
					
					4509 = {
						add_core = R12
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R12
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R12
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R12 religion = high_philosophy culture = rajnadhid }
					R12 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = {
						OR = { 
							R09 = { exists = yes }
							NOT = { 4467 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
						}
						OR = { 
							R12 = { exists = yes }
							NOT = { 4509 = { owned_by = ROOT } }
						}
					}
					
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								culture = shandibad
								culture = rajnadhid
								culture = sobhagand
								culture = muthadhaya
							}
						}
						add_core = R73
						every_neighbor_province = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R73
						}
						area = {
							limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
							add_core = R73
						}
					}
					release_with_religion_and_culture = { tag = R73 religion = high_philosophy culture = shandibad }
					R73 = { save_event_target_as = mage_rebel_nation }
				}
			}
			
			event_target:mage_rebel_nation = {
				override_country_name = THE_MANY_HANDS_REBELLION
				change_government = theocracy
				add_government_reform = magocracy_reform
				change_religion = high_philosophy
				
				capital_scope = {
					spawn_units_for = {
						amount = 22
						type = infantry
						who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
					}
					spawn_units_for = {
						amount = 4
						type = cavalry
						who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { mil_tech = 13 } }
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 10
							type = artillery
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { total_development = 1600 } }
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { infantry_in_province = event_target:mage_rebel_nation } }
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 18
							type = infantry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 4
							type = cavalry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						if = {
							limit = { ROOT = { mil_tech = 13 } }
							spawn_units_for = {
								amount = 8
								type = artillery
								who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { total_development = 2400 } }
					random_owned_province = {
						limit = { NOT = { infantry_in_province = event_target:mage_rebel_nation } }
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 12
							type = infantry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						spawn_units_for = {
							amount = 2
							type = cavalry
							who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
						}
						if = {
							limit = { ROOT = { mil_tech = 13 } }
							spawn_units_for = {
								amount = 6
								type = artillery
								who = event_target:mage_rebel_nation
							}
						}
					}
				}
					
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Chandra"
					dynasty = "of Many Hands"
					age = 28
					adm = 6
					dip = 2
					mil = 6
					culture = muthadhaya
					religion = high_philosophy
				}
				add_ruler_personality = mage_personality
				add_ruler_personality = intricate_web_weaver_personality
				add_ruler_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality
				define_ruler_to_general = {
					fire = 3
					shock = 11
					manuever = 4
					siege = 7
					trait = war_wizard_personality
				}
				
				set_ruler_flag = abjuration_3
				set_ruler_flag = abjuration_2
				set_ruler_flag = abjuration_1
				set_ruler_flag = conjuration_3
				set_ruler_flag = conjuration_2
				set_ruler_flag = conjuration_1
				set_ruler_flag = divination_3
				set_ruler_flag = divination_2
				set_ruler_flag = divination_1
				set_ruler_flag = enchantment_2
				set_ruler_flag = enchantment_1
				set_ruler_flag = evocation_3
				set_ruler_flag = evocation_2
				set_ruler_flag = evocation_1
				set_ruler_flag = illusion_1
				set_ruler_flag = necromancy_1
				set_ruler_flag = transmutation_2
				set_ruler_flag = transmutation_1
				set_ruler_flag = initialized_magic_flags
				
				# add_ruler_modifier = { name = witch_king_modifier duration = -1 }
				add_ruler_modifier = { name = command_chandra_of_many_hands duration = -1 }
				add_manpower = 60
				
				
				capital_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_fort_building_trigger = no }
						add_building = fort_15th
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = magic_realm_abjuration_empowered_ward
						duration = 1825
					}
				}
				
				declare_war_with_cb = {
					who = ROOT
					casus_belli = cb_civ_vs_monster
				}
				set_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.84.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
		tooltip = {
			event_target:mage_rebel_nation = {
				define_ruler = {
					name = "Chandra"
					dynasty = "of Many Hands"
					age = 28
					adm = 6
					dip = 2
					mil = 6

				}
				add_ruler_personality = mage_personality

				}
			}

country_event = { #Hidden annexation event, needs no loc
	id = the_command.90
	title = the_command.90.t
	desc = the_command.90.desc
	picture = LAND_MILITARY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		any_known_country = {
			has_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
			capital_scope = {
				controlled_by = ROOT
				has_siege = no
			}
			NOT = {
				war_score_against = {
					who = ROOT
					value = -50
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_known_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
				capital_scope = {
					controlled_by = ROOT
					has_siege = no
				}
				NOT = {
					war_score_against = {
						who = ROOT
						value = -50
					}
				}
			}
			restore_country_name = yes
			clr_country_flag = mage_rebel_nation
			ROOT = { inherit = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.90.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		
	}
}

country_event = { # Thunderfist Movement Menu
	id = the_command.100
	title = the_command.100.t
	desc = the_command.100.d
	picture = WESTERNISATION_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
			command_generate_move_target_canditates = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose first
		name = the_command.100.a
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_1
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				event_target:command_move_target_candidate_1 = {
					NOT = { is_core = R62 }
				}
			}
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_1
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_1
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose second
		name = the_command.100.b
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_2
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				event_target:command_move_target_candidate_2 = {
					NOT = { is_core = R62 }
				}
			}
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_2
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_2
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}

	option = { # Choose third
		name = the_command.100.c
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				event_target:command_move_target_candidate_3 = {
					NOT = { is_core = R62 }
				}
			}
		}
		goto = command_move_target_candidate_3
		
		command_move_orc_slave_state = {
			tag = R63
			target = command_move_target_candidate_3
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.100.dd
		highlight = yes
		
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_move_menu_open_flag
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		every_owned_province = {
			clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_1
			clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_2
			clr_province_flag = command_move_target_candidate_3
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			command_slave_state_cede_surrounding = { tag = R63 }
			command_slave_state_cede_surrounding = { tag = R63 }
		}
	}
}

	id = the_command.117
	title = the_command.117.t
	desc = the_command.117.desc
	picture = GENERALS_DISCUSSING_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			jadeforges_area = { cede_province = R66 add_core = R66 } #this makes it playable for MacOS. don't question it
			add_manpower = 10
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = three_commands_war_mod
				duration = 1825
			}
			capital_scope = {
				infantry = ROOT
			}
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = tag
				R94 = {
					while = {
						limit = { adm = 4 }
						change_adm = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { dip = 5 }
						change_dip = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { mil = 6 }
						change_mil = -1
					}
				}
				R95 = {
					while = {
						limit = { adm = 5 }
						change_dip = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { dip = 6 }
						change_mil = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { mil = 4 }
						change_mil = -1
					}
				}
				R96 = {
					while = {
						limit = { adm = 6 }
						change_mil = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { dip = 4 }
						change_adm = -1
					}
					while = {
						limit = { mil = 5 }
						change_mil = -1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.117.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		tooltip = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = three_commands_war_mod
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = R94 }
			set_ruler_culture = boar_command
			command_new_ruler_effect = { command = boar }
			add_treasury = 150
			add_manpower = 20
			capital_scope = {
				add_province_modifier = { name = boar_command_veteran_camp_tier_1 duration = -1 }
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
				infantry = ROOT
			}
			add_spy_network_in = {
				who = R95
				value = 100
			}
			add_spy_network_in = {
				who = R96
				value = 100
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = R95
				casus_belli = cb_three_commands
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = R96
				casus_belli = cb_three_commands
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = R95 }
			set_ruler_culture = lion_command
			command_new_ruler_effect = { command = lion }
			capital_scope = {
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
			}
			define_ruler_to_general = {
				fire = 4
				shock = 6
				manuever = 4
				siege = 4
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = R94
				casus_belli = cb_three_commands
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = R96
				casus_belli = cb_three_commands
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = R96 }
			set_ruler_culture = wolf_command
			command_new_ruler_effect = { command = wolf }
			add_treasury = 300
			add_mil_tech = 1
			capital_scope = {
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT
				cavalry = ROOT

				type = natural_scientist

	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { #new capital check
				R62 = {
					has_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_started
					all_war_enemy_countries = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north_punishment } }
							is_subject = yes

						}
					}
				}
			}
			R62 = { country_event = { id = the_command.126 } }
		}
	}

				R79 = { every_core_province = { limit = { owner = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } cede_province = R79 } R79 = { join_all_offensive_wars_of = R78 } }
				R80 = { every_core_province = { limit = { owner = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } cede_province = R80 } R80 = { join_all_offensive_wars_of = R78 } }

		}
	}
	option = {

		R62 = {

				type = cb_revolt_of_the_north_punishment
				months = 24
			}
			declare_war_with_cb = { who = ROOT casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north_punishment }
		}
	}

country_event = { #Sir revolt starts
	id = the_command.120

	desc = the_command.120.desc
	picture = IMPALED_SOLDIERS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = { #Special check for Rajnadhaga being a butt
			limit = { R09 = { exists = no } }
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_parraj_participation
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = the_command.121 days = 4380 } }
	}

	after = {
		R62 = {
			set_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_started

					}

						capital_scope = { add_province_modifier = { name = command_trade_power_for_ai duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { R62 = { has_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_oni_participation } }

				limit = { R62 = { alliance_with = Y01 } }
				Y01 = { country_event = { id = the_command.128 } }
			}
			else = { Y01 = { add_truce_with = R78 } }
		}
		4323 = { add_province_modifier = { name = command_defensiveness_for_ai duration = -1 } }
		4350 = { add_province_modifier = { name = command_defensiveness_for_ai duration = -1 } }

		4311 = { add_province_modifier = { name = command_trade_power_for_ai duration = -1 hidden = yes } }
		if = {
			limit = { #we don't need to put this up above because AI will never swap to Sir

					ai = yes
				}
			}

			4345 = { add_building = fort_15th add_province_modifier = { name = command_fake_fort duration = -1 } }
		}
	}

	option = { #DO NOT PUT THIS STUFF IN THE IMMEDIATE. WHITE PEACE IN THE IMMEDIATE CAUSES A CTD

				who = R62
				casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			R78 = {
				add_manpower = 10
			}
			4633 = {
				add_latest_building = { builder = R78 fort = yes }

				spawn_units_for = { type = cavalry who = R78 amount = 4 }

		}
		if = {

					}

				}

			}

					shock = 7

country_event = { #Offer for Truce
	id = the_command.121
	title = the_command.121.t
	desc = the_command.121.desc
	picture = LOOMING_DEATH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_in_war = {
			casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						all_war_enemy_countries = { #you won Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
							OR = {
								NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } }
								is_subject = yes
								capital_scope = { controller = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north defenders = THIS } } }
							}
						}
						AND = { #you lost Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
							4630 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
							4538 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
							4311 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = the_command.3003 }
			}
		}
	}

	#this currently always results in White Peace after 10 years.
	#In the future it could be warscore dependent,
	#but rn the is_in_war war_score trigger is bugged and doesn't work
	option = {
		name = the_command.121.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		custom_tooltip = command_sir_revolt_truce_offer_tt
		R78 = { country_event = { id = the_command.122 days = 31 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.121.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_prestige = 1
	}
}
country_event = { #Truce Offer P2
	id = the_command.122
	title = the_command.122.t
	desc = the_command.122.desc
	picture = LOOMING_DEATH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes

	trigger = {
		is_in_war = {
			casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.122.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}

		R62 = {
			if = { limit = { ai = yes } set_capital = 4630 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership }
				remove_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -10
			}
			set_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_victory
			every_war_enemy_country = {
				limit = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } }
				capital_scope = {
					remove_province_modifier = command_defensiveness_for_ai
					remove_province_modifier = command_trade_power_for_ai
				}
			}
			every_war_enemy_country = { #yes you have to do it like this
				limit = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } }
				white_peace = R62
			}
			every_known_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = sir_revolt_fake_truce_flag }
				clr_country_flag = sir_revolt_fake_truce_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_started
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_xia_participation
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_oni_participation
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_rebel_participation
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_khadisrapur_participation
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_sarnavan_participation
			clr_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_parraj_participation
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			4323 = { remove_province_modifier = command_defensiveness_for_ai }
			4350 = { remove_province_modifier = command_defensiveness_for_ai }
			4521 = { remove_province_modifier = command_defensiveness_for_ai }
			4628 = { remove_province_modifier = command_defensiveness_for_ai }
			4630 = { remove_province_modifier = command_trade_power_for_ai }
			4538 = { remove_province_modifier = command_trade_power_for_ai }
			4311 = { remove_province_modifier = command_trade_power_for_ai }
			4352 = { remove_building = fort_15th remove_province_modifier = command_fake_fort }
			4345 = { remove_building = fort_15th remove_province_modifier = command_fake_fort }
		}
		Y01 = { remove_country_modifier = command_aingjada_elsewhere }
		shamakhad_region = {
			limit = { NOT = { R62 = { owns_or_subject_of = PREV } } }
			remove_province_modifier = command_shamakhadi_resistance
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.122.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		
		add_prestige = 1
	}
}

					amount = 5 #The effect needs to be weirdly written to avoid going over string limit
					effect = "
						random_owned_province = {
							limit = {
								region = shamakhad_region
								culture_is_hobgoblin = no
								NOT = { has_province_modifier = hobgoblin_minority_integrated_large }
							}
							generic_add_race_minority_size_effect = { race = hobgoblin }
						}
					"
				}
				shamakhad_region = {
					limit = { owner = { OR = { tag = R62 is_subject_of = R62 } } }
					add_permanent_province_modifier = {
						name = command_end_of_soft_words
						duration = 18250
					}
				}
			}			
		}
	}
}

	}

			country_event = { id = the_command.311 }
		}
	}

		name = flavor_castanor_go_back

				1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }

			}

				limit = {

							template = merc_command_wolf_army

		}
	}

				country_event = { id = the_command.318 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_hired_mercenary_company = {
							template = merc_command_dragon_army
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = command_army_not_hired_tt
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Elephant
		name = the_command.310.e
		trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = command_armies_elephant_menu_open }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = command_armies_main_menu_open
				5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				country_event = { id = the_command.320 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_hired_mercenary_company = {
							template = merc_command_elephant_army
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = command_army_not_hired_tt
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Tiger
		name = the_command.310.f
		trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = command_armies_tiger_menu_open }
			}
			hidden_effect = {

				6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }

			estate = estate_dragon_command

		}
		set_estate_privilege = estate_dragon_command_land_rights

			remove_estate_privilege = estate_wolf_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_lion_command_act_of_division

			remove_estate_privilege = estate_elephant_command_act_of_division
			remove_estate_privilege = estate_tiger_command_act_of_division
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = the_command.999
	title = the_command.999.t
	desc = the_command.999.desc

		}

	}
	option = { #equipment shortages, who gets priority?

			factor = 1
		}

country_event = {
	id = the_command.1000
	title = the_command.1000.t
	desc = the_command.1000.desc
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					kanzad_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_51_53_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					grozumdihr_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					ovdal_az_an_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_57_59_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					hul_az_krakazol_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
					dwarovrod_63_65_area = { type = all is_city = yes }
				}
				set_country_flag = command_tree_of_stone_campaign_unlocked_flag
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { ai = yes }
				set_country_flag = estate_wolf_command_present_agenda generate_estate_agenda = estate_wolf_command
				set_country_flag = estate_boar_command_present_agenda generate_estate_agenda = estate_boar_command
				set_country_flag = estate_lion_command_present_agenda generate_estate_agenda = estate_lion_command
			}
			else = {
				pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
				pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
				pick_random_estate_if_present = { flag = present_agenda estate_action = generate_estate_agenda }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = estate_wolf_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_boar_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_lion_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_dragon_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_elephant_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_tiger_command_present_agenda
		clr_country_flag = estate_gerunanin_present_agenda
		clear_estate_agenda_cache = ROOT
		
		clr_country_flag = disable_first_lion_command_agenda_flag
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.1000.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = estate_wolf_command_present_agenda
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					command_has_potential_campaign = yes
					command_has_available_wolf_campaign = no
				}
			}
		}
		start_estate_agenda = estate_wolf_command
		goto = estate_wolf_command
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = { #Disable regular logic for Azjakuma campaign
					NOT = { has_country_flag = command_azjakuma_campaign_unlocked_flag }
					has_country_flag = command_azjakuma_campaign_completed_flag
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = command_xiadao_campaign_completed_flag }
					AND = { #Xiadao into Shamakhad + Bianfang = first three wars
						has_country_flag = command_shamakhad_campaign_completed_flag
						NOT = { has_country_flag = command_bianfang_campaign_completed_flag }
					}
					AND = { #Dhujat + Xianjie + Yanszin/Zyujyut are the next three wars
						has_country_flag = command_dhujat_campaign_completed_flag
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = command_xianjie_campaign_completed_flag }
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = command_yanszin_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_zyujyut_campaign_completed_flag
							}
						}
					}
					AND = { #Ghavaanaj/Rakhadesh + Telebei + Sikai + Zyujyut/Yanszin are the next four wars
						has_country_flag = command_sikai_campaign_completed_flag
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = command_yanszin_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_zyujyut_campaign_completed_flag
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = command_rakhadesh_campaign_completed_flag
									has_country_flag = command_ghavaanaj_campaign_completed_flag
								}
							}
						}
					}
					AND = { #Ghavaanaj/Rakhadesh + Dhenbasana/Bhuvauri + Hukai + Baihon Xinh/Thidinkai + Tianlou next five wars
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = command_baihon_xinh_campaign_completed_flag
							has_country_flag = command_thidinkai_campaign_completed_flag
						}
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = command_dhenbasana_campaign_completed_flag
							has_country_flag = command_bhuvauri_campaign_completed_flag
						}
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = command_tianlou_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_hukai_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_rakhadesh_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_ghavaanaj_campaign_completed_flag
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.1000.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = estate_boar_command_present_agenda
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					command_has_potential_campaign = yes
					command_has_available_boar_campaign = no
				}
			}
		}
		start_estate_agenda = estate_boar_command
		goto = estate_boar_command
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { #Xiadao into Shamakhad + Bianfang = first three wars
						has_country_flag = command_xiadao_campaign_completed_flag
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = command_shamakhad_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_bianfang_campaign_completed_flag
							}
						}
					}
					AND = { #Dhujat + Xianjie + Yanszin/Zyujyut are the next three wars
						has_country_flag = command_xianjie_campaign_completed_flag
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = command_yanszin_campaign_completed_flag
							has_country_flag = command_zyujyut_campaign_completed_flag
						}
						NOT = { has_country_flag = command_dhujat_campaign_completed_flag }
					}
					AND = { #Ghavaanaj/Rakhadesh + Telebei + Sikai + Zyujyut/Yanszin are the next four wars
						has_country_flag = command_telebei_campaign_completed_flag
						has_country_flag = command_zyujyut_campaign_completed_flag
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = command_rakhadesh_campaign_completed_flag
							has_country_flag = command_ghavaanaj_campaign_completed_flag
						}
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = command_yanszin_campaign_completed_flag
						}
					}
					AND = { #Ghavaanaj/Rakhadesh + Dhenbasana/Bhuvauri + Hukai + Baihon Xinh/Thidinkai + Tianlou next five wars
						has_country_flag = command_rakhadesh_campaign_completed_flag
						has_country_flag = command_hukai_campaign_completed_flag
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = command_dhenbasana_campaign_completed_flag
							has_country_flag = command_bhuvauri_campaign_completed_flag
						}
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_country_flag = command_tianlou_campaign_completed_flag
								has_country_flag = command_ghavaanaj_campaign_completed_flag
								OR = {
									has_country_flag = command_baihon_xinh_campaign_completed_flag
									has_country_flag = command_thidinkai_campaign_completed_flag
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.1000.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = estate_lion_command_present_agenda
			NOT = {

					command_has_potential_campaign = yes

							has_country_flag = command_yanszin_campaign_completed_flag

	title = the_command.1001.t

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
		has_country_flag = command_war_room
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {

country_event = { #dispute over governance of newly conquered territories, who gets priority?
	id = the_command.1002
	title = the_command.1002.t 
	desc = the_command.1002.desc
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
		has_country_flag = command_war_room
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } } }

				}
				1 = {

					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {

				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Mediate in marriage negotiations
	id = the_command.1004
	title = the_command.1004.t 
	desc = the_command.1004.desc 
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
		has_country_flag = command_war_room
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } } }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } } }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } } }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } } }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } } }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1004.a
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = 10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } }

		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command

		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 5 } }
			#effects for estate_tiger_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_tiger_command
				loyalty = -5
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 6 } }
			#effects for estate_elephant_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_elephant_command
				loyalty = -5
			}
		}
		
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 5 }
		add_absolutism = 5
	}
}

country_event = { #A high level murder
	id = the_command.1007
	title = the_command.1007.t 
	desc = the_command.1007.desc 
	picture = NOBLE_ESTATE_DEMANDS_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_reform = hobgoblin_stratocracy_reform
		has_country_flag = command_war_room
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command}
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_1 }
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_wolf_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } } }
					1 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_boar_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } } }
					2 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_lion_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } } }
					3 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_dragon_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } } }
					4 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_tiger_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } } }
					5 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
				1 = {
					trigger = { has_estate = estate_elephant_command NOT = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } } }
					6 = { save_event_target_as = command_war_room_estate_2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1007.a
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_dragon_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 5 } }
			#effects for estate_tiger_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_tiger_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_1 = { province_id = 6 } }
			#effects for estate_elephant_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_elephant_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		
		kill_leader = { type = general }
		add_army_tradition = -5
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 5 }
	}
	option = { 
		name = the_command.1007.b
		
		if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 1 } }
			#effects for estate_wolf_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_wolf_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 2 } }
			#effects for estate_boar_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_boar_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 3 } }
			#effects for estate_lion_command
			add_estate_loyalty = {
				estate = estate_lion_command
				loyalty = -10
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { event_target:command_war_room_estate_2 = { province_id = 4 } }
			#effects for estate_dragon_command

##############################################
###   The Great Insubordination Disaster   ###

#starts the tickup
country_event = {
	id = the_command.1984
	title = the_command.1984.t
	desc = the_command.1984.d
	picture = BAD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = R62
		mission_completed = R62_the_jade_march
		if = {
			limit = { ai = no }
			has_estate = estate_tiger_command
			has_estate = estate_dragon_command
			has_estate = estate_elephant_command
		}
		else = {
			OR = {
				has_estate = estate_tiger_command
				has_estate = estate_dragon_command
				has_estate = estate_elephant_command
			}
		}
		# Requires each subcontinent to have 30 provinces owned + over 120 provinces outside of Shamakhad.
		if = {
			limit = { ai = yes }
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 40
				superregion = yanshen_superregion
			}
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 40
				superregion = south_haless_superregion
			}
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 40
				superregion = rahen_superregion
				NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
			}
		}
		else = {
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 30
				superregion = yanshen_superregion
			}
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 30
				superregion = south_haless_superregion
			}
			num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
				value = 30
				superregion = rahen_superregion
				NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
			}
		}
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = { value = 120 NOT = { region = shamakhad_region } }
		
		rahen_superregion = {
			NOT = { region = shamakhad_region }
			has_terrain = city_terrain
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = R62
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = R63
							tag = R64
						}
						is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = { who = R62 type = slave_state }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		yanshen_superregion = {
			has_terrain = city_terrain
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = R62
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = R63
							tag = R64
						}
						is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = { who = R62 type = slave_state }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		south_haless_superregion = {
			OR = {
				has_terrain = city_terrain
				province_id = 4559
				province_id = 4565
			}
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = R62
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = R63
							tag = R64
						}
						is_subject_of_type_with_overlord = { who = R62 type = slave_state }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = insubordination_start_flag
			set_country_flag = insubordination_be_nice
			if = {
				limit = { ai = yes }
				set_global_flag = ai_insubordination
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = the_command.1984.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_tooltip = command_1984_tt
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -10
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = command_estate_pain
			duration = -1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = the_command.1976 days = 180 random = 365 }	#Oni Unrest
			country_event = { id = the_command.1980 days = 45 random = 30 }		#Tiger Command War Room Input
			country_event = { id = the_command.1981 days = 180 random = 30 }	#Elephant Command War Room Input
			country_event = { id = the_command.1982 days = 295 random = 30 }	#Dragon Command War Room Input
			country_event = { id = the_command.1985 days = 450 random = 60 }	#Boar Command vs Dragon Command
			country_event = { id = the_command.1986 days = 580 random = 60 }	#Wolf Command vs Elephant Command
			country_event = { id = the_command.1987 days = 720 random = 60 }	#Lion Command vs Tiger Command
		}
	}
}

country_event = {		# oni revolt
	id = the_command.1977
	title = the_command.1977.t
	desc = the_command.1977.d
	picture = ONI_THINK_HOBGOBLIN_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		Y01 = { is_subject_of_type = slave_state }
		ai = no
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			Y01 = {
				white_peace = R67
				white_peace = R68
				white_peace = R69
				every_owned_province = { # delete the forts
					limit = { fort_level = 2 }
					remove_building = fort_15th
					remove_building = fort_16th
					remove_building = fort_17th
					remove_building = fort_18th
				}
				every_owned_province = { # add back the forts
					limit = {
						OR = {
							province_id = 4833
							province_id = 4831
							province_id = 5430
							province_id = 4829
							province_id = 4828
							province_id = 4901
							province_id = 4813
						}
					}
					add_latest_building = { builder = Y01 fort = yes }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_insubordination_fort
						duration = 31
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.1977.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 15 }
		Y01 = {
			declare_war_with_cb = {
				who = R62
				casus_belli = cb_insubordination
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.1977.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		add_stability = -1
		add_legitimacy = -10
		Y01 = {
			grant_independence = yes
			reverse_add_casus_belli = {
				target = R62
				type = cb_vassalize_mission
				months = 300
			}
		}
	}
}

		random_owned_province = { limit = { fort_level = 2 NOT = { has_province_modifier = command_elephant_fortified_provinces } superregion = south_haless_superregion } add_province_modifier = { name = command_elephant_fortified_provinces duration = 1825 } }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_elephant_command
			loyalty = 5
		}
	}
	option = {		# flat out no
		name = the_command.1981.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_elephant_command

					days = 31

				every_owned_province = { # delete the forts
					limit = { fort_level = 2 }
					remove_building = fort_15th
					remove_building = fort_16th
					remove_building = fort_17th
					remove_building = fort_18th
				}
				every_owned_province = { # add back the forts
					limit = {
						OR = {
							province_id = 4826
							province_id = 4843
							province_id = 4842
							province_id = 4951
							province_id = 4982
							province_id = 4851
							province_id = 4846
							province_id = 4976
							province_id = 4859
							province_id = 4841
							province_id = 4884
							province_id = 4886
							province_id = 4879
							province_id = 4896
							province_id = 4874
							province_id = 4930
							province_id = 4876
							province_id = 4868
							province_id = 4871
							province_id = 4914
							province_id = 4911
							province_id = 4979
							province_id = 4919
							province_id = 4925
							province_id = 4923
							AND = {
								is_capital = yes
								has_global_flag = ai_insubordination
							}
						}
						NOT = { fort_level = 2 }
					}
					add_latest_building = { builder = R69 fort = yes }
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = command_insubordination_fort
						duration = 1825
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ai_insubordination } }
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = command_capital_stronghold_t1
							duration = -1
						}
						add_base_production = 2000
					}
					set_province_flag = command_dragon_capital_flag
					random_neighbor_province = {
						limit = {
							has_terrain = farmlands
							owned_by = R69
						}
						add_province_modifier= {
							name = command_dragon_warcamp
							duration = -1
						}
						set_province_flag = command_dragon_warcamp
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = the_command.1993.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

	option = {
		name = flavor_castanor_go_back
		highlight = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = command_insubordination_menu_open_flag
			if = {
				limit = { ai = yes }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = command_insubordination_menu_ai_cooldown
					duration = 365
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
	}
}

country_event = { # Fall of the Tiger Command
	id = the_command.1994
	title = the_command.1994.t
	desc = the_command.1994.d
	picture = FAMINE_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = the_command.1994.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_tooltip = command_1994_tt

		set_country_flag = R62_tiger_subdued

		R67 = { kill_ruler = yes }
		event_target:tiger_command_capital = { add_base_tax = -2 add_base_production = -2 add_base_manpower = -2 }
		add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		add_legitimacy_or_monarch_power = { VAL = 20 }

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership }
			remove_country_modifier = command_exemplary_leadership
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_respected_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_modifier = command_respected_leadership }
			remove_country_modifier = command_respected_leadership
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_legendary_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = command_legendary_leadership } }
			add_ruler_modifier = {
				name = command_exemplary_leadership
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_mil_power = 50
		}
		
		custom_tooltip = command_1994_2_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			R67 = {
				disband_all_units = yes
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = command_tiger_warcamp }
					clr_province_flag = command_tiger_warcamp
				}
				if = {
					limit = { owns = 4504 }
					4504 = { set_province_flag = command_tiger_warcamp }
				}
			}
			# Remove capital mechanics
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = ai_insubordination } }
				event_target:tiger_command_capital = {
					add_base_production = -2000
					remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t1
					remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t2
					remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t3
					remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t4
				}
			}
			inherit = R67
		}
	}
}

country_event = {	# encirclement breaks if you stop controlling all neighbor provinces
	id = the_command.2001
	title = the_command.2001.t
	desc = the_command.2001.d
	picture = SIEGE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:tiger_command_capital = {
						has_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
						any_neighbor_province = {
							NOT = { controller = { OR = { tag = R62 alliance_with = R62 is_subject_of = R62 } } }
							owner = { OR = { offensive_war_with = R62 defensive_war_with = R62 } }
						}
					}
				}
				R67 = { command_strengthen_capital = yes }
				event_target:tiger_command_capital = { clr_province_flag  = command_encircled_flag }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:elephant_command_capital = {
						has_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
						any_neighbor_province = {
							NOT = { controller = { OR = { tag = R62 alliance_with = R62 is_subject_of = R62 } } }
							owner = { OR = { offensive_war_with = R62 defensive_war_with = R62 } }
						}
					}
				}
				R68 = { command_strengthen_capital = yes }
				event_target:elephant_command_capital = { clr_province_flag  = command_encircled_flag }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:dragon_command_capital = {
						has_province_flag = command_encircled_flag
						any_neighbor_province = {
							NOT = { controller = { OR = { tag = R62 alliance_with = R62 is_subject_of = R62 } } }
							owner = { OR = { offensive_war_with = R62 defensive_war_with = R62 } }
						}
					}
				}
				R69 = { command_strengthen_capital = yes }
				event_target:dragon_command_capital = { clr_province_flag  = command_encircled_flag }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.2001.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_tooltip = command_2001_tt
	}
}

			}

				}
			}
		}

				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t3
				remove_province_modifier = command_capital_stronghold_t4
				clr_province_flag = command_destroyed_logistics_flag
				clr_province_flag = command_encircled_flag

				tiltaghar_area = {
					limit = { owner = { OR = { tag = R62 is_subject_of = R62 } } }

					add_core = R67
				}
