			white_peace = R69
			R67 = { grant_independence = yes }
			R68 = { grant_independence = yes }
			R69 = { grant_independence = yes }
		}
	}

country_event = { #Force Command AI to do stuff
	id = the_command.3002
	title = the_command.3002.t
	desc = the_command.3002.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				R67 = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				R68 = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				R69 = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.3002.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		command_force_progress_campaign_multiple_effect = yes
		random_owned_province = { #build forts dummy
			limit = {
				has_terrain = city_terrain
				has_fort_building_trigger = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = { R62 = { mil_tech = 24 } }
				add_building_construction = { building = fort_18th speed = 1 cost = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R62 = { mil_tech = 19 } }
				add_building_construction = { building = fort_17th speed = 1 cost = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { R62 = { mil_tech = 14 } }
				add_building_construction = { building = fort_16th speed = 1 cost = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				add_building_construction = { building = fort_15th speed = 1 cost = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				adm_tech = 8
			}
			every_owned_province = { #build courthouses dummy (Command needs them for korashi + gov cap)
				limit = { has_courthouse_building_trigger = no }
				random = {
					chance = 25
					if = {
						limit = { R62 = { adm_tech = 22 } }
						add_building_construction = {
							building = town_hall
							speed = 1
							cost = 1
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_building_construction = {
							building = courthouse
							speed = 1
							cost = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Debug event that triggers every year
	id = the_command.3003
	title = the_command.3003.t
	desc = the_command.3003.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = R62
		OR = {
			AND = { #Insubordination won via unconditional surrender
				has_country_flag = insubordination_active_flag
				OR = {
					R67 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } }
					R68 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } }
					R69 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } }
				}
			}
			AND = { #Sir Revolt bugtest
				has_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_started
				OR = {
					all_war_enemy_countries = { #you won Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
						OR = {
							NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } }
							is_subject = yes
							capital_scope = { controller = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north defenders = THIS } } }
						}
					}
					AND = { #you lost Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
						4630 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
						4538 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
						4311 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = the_command.3003.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		if = { #Calm Down Sir
			limit = { has_country_flag = command_sir_revolt_started }
			if = {
				limit = { #You won Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
					all_war_enemy_countries = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north } }
							is_subject = yes
							capital_scope = { controller = { is_in_war = { casus_belli = cb_revolt_of_the_north defenders = THIS } } }
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = the_command.126 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { #You lost Sir Revolt due to unconditional surrender
					4630 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
					4538 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
					4311 = { NOT = { controlled_by = R62 } }
				}
				country_event = { id = the_command.123 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = insubordination_active_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { R67 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } } }
				country_event = { id = the_command.1994 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { R68 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } } }
				country_event = { id = the_command.1995 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { R69 = { capital_scope = { controlled_by = R62 } } }
				country_event = { id = the_command.1996 }
			}
		}
	}
}
